\end{DoxyReturn}

Set the Access Point Name (A\+P\+N) for the given profile.

The A\+P\+N must be an A\+S\+C\+I\+I string.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+K on success
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+B\+A\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+E\+R if an input parameter is not valid
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+L\+T if the data session is currently connected for the given profile
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If A\+P\+N is too long (max A\+P\+N\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+L\+E\+N digits), it is a fatal error, the function will not return. 

The process exits, if an invalid profile object is given 
\end{DoxyNote}

\item[{const char $\ast$}]{password}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{le__mdc__interface_8h_abf58f1dd7d4f9b915647e9c0f642065b}
Set authentication property

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+K on success
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The process exits, if user\+Name or password are N\+U\+L\+L when type is not P\+A\+\_\+\+M\+D\+C\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+H\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+E
\item The process exits, if an invalid profile object is given 
\end{DoxyItemize}

If user\+Name is too long (max U\+S\+E\+R\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+L\+E\+N digits), it is a fatal error, the function will not return. 

If password is too long (max P\+A\+S\+S\+W\+O\+R\+D\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+L\+E\+N digits), it is a fatal error, the function will not return. 
\end{DoxyNote}
